## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: chemical reaction kinetics (mass-action rate laws / reaction engineering ODE models)
**Analysis**: The target dA_dt is an ordinary differential equation describing the time-rate of change of a chemical species concentration A. With only (t, A) available, the most common kinetics are single-species lumped rate laws (mass-action orders, reversible relaxation to equilibrium, autocatalysis/inhibition) possibly with explicit time-dependent rate coefficients.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Zero-order consumption: dA_dt = -c0 (rate independent of A; surface-limited or excess-reactant regime)
- First-order decay (mass-action): dA_dt = -c0 * A (unimolecular decay, pseudo-first-order when other reactants are constant)
- Second-order decay: dA_dt = -c0 * A**2 (bimolecular self-reaction or approximation when two equal concentrations react)
- n-th order (power-law) kinetics: dA_dt = -c0 * A**c1 (empirical/non-integer reaction order, complex mechanisms)
- Reversible first-order to equilibrium: dA_dt = -c0 * (A - c1) (relaxation toward equilibrium concentration c1)
- Parallel pathways (sum of orders): dA_dt = -(c0 * A + c1 * A**2) (competing unimolecular and bimolecular loss channels)
- Autocatalytic term: dA_dt = c0 * A - c1 * A**2 (self-amplifying production with quadratic depletion; simple autocatalysis model form)
- Rational saturation/inhibition in effective rate: dA_dt = -c0 * A / (A + c1) (rate saturates at high A; transport/coverage limitation)
- Self-inhibition (product/aggregation-like): dA_dt = -c0 * A / (1 + c1 * A) (increasing A suppresses effective rate)
- Time-dependent rate coefficient (catalyst deactivation/aging): dA_dt = -c0 * exp(-c1 * t) * A (apparent first-order with decaying activity over time)
- Induction/activation period: dA_dt = -c0 * (1 - exp(-c1 * t)) * A (rate turns on gradually from near-zero)
- Stretched-exponential (dispersed kinetics) rate form: dA_dt = -c0 * t**c1 * A (time-dependent apparent rate due to heterogeneity or changing environment)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Mass-action single-step consumption typically gives dA_dt proportional to A**n; the exponent indicates effective reaction order.
- If dA_dt remains finite/nonzero as A -> 0, a zero-order term (constant source/sink) is implicated.
- Relaxation toward a nonzero steady concentration is often captured by a driving-force form (A - c), yielding dA_dt -> 0 as A -> c.
- Competing mechanisms commonly appear as additive loss terms (e.g., c0*A + c1*A**2), producing curvature changes in dA_dt vs A.
- Plateauing of |dA_dt| at high A suggests rational saturation forms like A/(A + c) (coverage/transport limitation).
- Decreasing reaction activity over time (catalyst deactivation, fouling) is naturally modeled by a multiplicative exp(-c*t) factor on a base rate law.
- Induction/activation periods (e.g., warming-up, initiator buildup) are indicated by multiplicative (1 - exp(-c*t)) factors that start near 0 and approach 1.
- Sign changes in dA_dt over time or with A can indicate reversible behavior or autocatalytic production plus depletion terms.
- Non-integer powers or explicit t**c scaling in the rate can represent heterogeneous/distributed kinetics or evolving microstructure rather than a single elementary step.

Final search results

Best expression     : A*c0*exp(c1*t) + A*c2/(A*c3 + c4) + c5*sin(A*c6 + c7) + c8/(A*c3 + c4)
Structure desc      : Additive form combining A·exp(c1 t), a rational-in-A term with shared denominator (A*c3+c4), a sinusoid in A, and another 1/(A*c3+c4) term. t only enters the exponential; A enters the rational denominator and sine argument. For large A, A*c2/(A*c3+c4) tends to c2/c3≈-216 (dominant offset), while c8/(A*c3+c4) decays like O(1/A); the sine amplitude is huge (c5≈217) so oscillations dominate around that offset. Approximate: -0.547A·e^{-0.037t} -216 +217·sin(0.0691A+1.595) (plus a small -190/(1.085A+0.880)).
Fitted params       : c0=-5.4752e-01, c1=-3.7079e-02, c2=-2.3429e+02, c3=1.0850e+00, c4=8.7977e-01, c5=2.1701e+02, c6=6.9090e-02, c7=1.5951e+00, c8=-1.9024e+02
Train NMSE          : 3.58e-13
Test NMSE           : 3.51e-13
OOD Test NMSE       : 2.64e-09

============================================================
GT Equivalence Verification (CRK3)
============================================================
GT: -c0*A**c1 - c2*A*exp(-c3*_s*t) + c4*_w*cos(log(A + c5))
Candidate formulas: 65

GT is the fixed function of two variables \(t,A\):
\[
f(t,A)= -0.5475\,A^2\;-\;0.5475\,A\,e^{-0.037079\,t}\;+\;0.704922\,\cos(\log(A+1)).
\]
So any matching candidate must be able (by choosing its free constants) to reproduce **simultaneously**:
1) a pure polynomial term \(\propto A^2\) with coefficient \(-0.5475\) (independent of \(t\)),
2) a term \(\propto A e^{kt}\) with \(k=-0.037079\) and coefficient \(-0.5475\),
3) a term exactly \(\propto \cos(\log(A+1))\) with coefficient \(0.704922\),
and **no extra functional dependence** (no rational-in-\(A\) leftovers, no \(\sin(\cdot)\), no \(\log(\cdot)\) instead of \(\cos(\log(\cdot))\), etc.).

Below, for each candidate, I check whether its available function “basis” can be tuned to exactly these three components.

---

### 1. \(A c0 e^{c1 t} + \frac{A c2}{A c3+c4} + c5\sin(Ac6+c7) + \frac{c8}{A c3+c4}\)
Has \(A e^{c1 t}\) (good for the exponential-in-\(t\) term), but the other terms are rational in \(A\) and \(\sin(\text{linear }A)\). Cannot produce \(A^2\) nor \(\cos(\log(A+1))\). **No match**.

### 2. Candidate 1 + constant \(c9\)
Adding a constant doesn’t help create \(A^2\) or \(\cos(\log(A+1))\). **No match**.

### 3. \(A c0 e^{c1 t} + A c2 + \frac{A}{A c3+c4} + A^{c5}c6 + c7\)
Can make \(A^{c5}c6\) into \(-0.5475 A^2\) by setting \(c5=2, c6=-0.5475\). Can make \(A c0 e^{c1 t}\) into \(-0.5475 A e^{-0.037079 t}\) by setting \(c1=-0.037079, c0=-0.5475\).  
But there is **no way** to get \(\cos(\log(A+1))\); only linear \(A\), rational, and power terms. **No match**.

### 4. \(A c0 e^{c1 t} + A c2 + \frac{A c3}{A c4+c5} + A^{c6}c7 + c8\)
Same issue as (3): can fit \(A e^{kt}\) and \(A^2\), but no \(\cos(\log(A+1))\). **No match**.

### 5. \(A^2 c0 + A c1 e^{c2 t} + A c3 + \frac{A c4}{A c5+c6} + \frac{c7}{A c5+c6} + c8\)
Has \(A^2\) and \(A e^{c2 t}\) (good), but remaining terms are linear/rational/constant; cannot form \(\cos(\log(A+1))\). **No match**.

### 6. \(A c0 e^{c1 t} + A c2 + \frac{A c3}{A c4+c5} + A^{c6}c7 + \frac{c8}{A c4+c5} + c9\)
No \(\cos(\log(A+1))\). **No match**.

### 7. \(A c0 e^{c1 t} + A c2 + \frac{A c3}{A c4+c5} + c6\log(A c7+1) + c8\)
Has \(\log(\cdot)\) but GT needs \(\cos(\log(\cdot))\). A linear combination of \(\log(Ac7+1)\), rational, and polynomial/exponential terms cannot equal \(\cos(\log(A+1))\) for all \(A\). **No match**.

### 8. \(A c0 e^{c1 t} + A c2 + c3 + c4 e^{A c5} + c6 e^{A c7}\)
No \(A^2\) term and no \(\cos(\log(A+1))\). **No match**.

### 9. \(A c0 e^{c1 t} + A c2 + A^{c3}c4 + \frac{c5 t}{A c6+c7} + \frac{c8}{A c6+c7} + c9\)
Can make \(A^{c3}c4\) into \(A^2\), and \(A c0 e^{c1 t}\) into the \(A e^{kt}\) term, but no \(\cos(\log(A+1))\). Also has \(t/(A\cdot +)\) structure unless zeroed. **No match**.

### 10. \(A^2 c0 + A c1 e^{c2 t} + A c3 + \frac{c4 t}{A c5+c6} + \frac{c7}{A c5+c6} + c8\)
No \(\cos(\log(A+1))\). **No match**.

### 11. Candidate 7 plus \(\frac{c8}{A c4+c5}+c9\)
Still only \(\log(\cdot)\), not \(\cos(\log(\cdot))\). **No match**.

### 12. \(A c0 e^{c1 t} + A c2 + A^{c3}c4 + c5\log(A c6+1) + c7\)
Has \(\log\) but not \(\cos(\log)\). **No match**.

### 13. \(A^2 c0 + A c1 e^{c2 t} + A c3 + A c4 + c5 + c6\log(A c7+1)\)
Again \(\log\) not \(\cos(\log)\). **No match**.

### 14. \(A^2 c0 + A c1 e^{c2 t} + A c3 + c4\log(A c5+1) + c6\)
Same issue. **No match**.

### 15. \(A c0 e^{c1 t} + A c2 + A^{c3}c4 + A^{c5}c6 + c7\)
Can make one power term be \(A^2\), but no \(\cos(\log(A+1))\). **No match**.

### 16. \(\frac{A c0}{A c1+c2} + c3\sin(Ac4+c5) + c6\sqrt{A^2+c7}e^{c8 t} + \frac{c9}{A c1+c2}\)
Wrong functional forms: rational-in-\(A\), \(\sin(\text{linear }A)\), \(\sqrt{A^2+\cdot}e^{c8 t}\). Cannot equal polynomial \(A^2\) plus \(\cos(\log(A+1))\). **No match**.

### 17. \(A^2 c0 + A c1 e^{c2 t} + A c3 + c4\sin(c5 t+c6) + c7\log(A c8+1) + c9\)
Has \(\log\) not \(\cos(\log)\), and also \(\sin(\text{linear }t)\) unless killed. **No match**.

### 18. \(A c0 + A^{c1}c2 + c3 + c4\log(A c5+1) + c6\sqrt{A^2+c7}e^{c8 t}\)
No \(\cos(\log)\), and exponential-in-\(t\) term has \(\sqrt{A^2+\cdot}\), not \(A\). **No match**.

### 19. \(A^2 c0 + A c1 + c2 + c3\log(A c4+1) + c5\sqrt{A^2+c6}e^{c7 t}\)
No \(\cos(\log)\); wrong \(t\)-dependence factor in \(A\). **No match**.

### 20. \(A^2 c0 + A c1 e^{c2 t} + A c3 + c4 e^{c5 t} + c6\log(A c7+1) + c8\)
Has \(\log\) not \(\cos(\log)\). Also extra \(e^{c5 t}\) term unless zeroed. **No match**.

### 21. \(A^2 c0 + A c1 e^{c2 t} + A c3 + c4\log(c5 t+1) + c6\log(A c7+1) + c8\)
Still \(\log\) not \(\cos(\log)\). **No match**.

### 22. \(A^2 c0 + A c1 e^{c2 t} + A c3 + c4 t^{c5} + c6\log(A c7+1) + c8\)
Still \(\log\) not \(\cos(\log)\). **No match**.

### 23. \(A^2 c0 + A c1 e^{c2 t} + A c3 + A c4(c5+t)^{c6} + c7\log(A c8+1) + c9\)
Still \(\log\) not \(\cos(\log)\). **No match**.

### 24. \(A^2 c0 + A c1 e^{c2 t} + A c3 + c4 + c5\log(A c6+1) + c7 t\)
Still \(\log\) not \(\cos(\log)\). **No match**.

### 25. \(A c0 e^{c1 t} + A c2 + \frac{A}{A c3+c4} + c5\sin(Ac6+c7) + c8\)
No \(\cos(\log)\). **No match**.

### 26. \(A c0 e^{c1 t} + A c2(c3+t)^{c4} + c5 + c6 e^{A c7} + c8 e^{A c9}\)
No \(A^2\) and no \(\cos(\log)\). **No match**.

### 27. \(A c0 e^{c1 t} + c2 + c3\log(A c4+1) + c5 e^{A c6} + c7(A+c8)^2\)
Has quadratic \((A+c8)^2\) (can yield \(A^2\) plus linear/constant pieces), and has \(A e^{c1 t}\). But the nonpolynomial \(A\)-term is \(\log(\cdot)\), not \(\cos(\log(\cdot))\). **No match**.

### 28. \(A c0 e^{c1 t} + c2\sin(A c3+c4) + c5 e^{A c6} + c7\)
No \(A^2\), no \(\cos(\log)\). **No match**.

I need to compare each candidate against the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT:** `-0.5475*A² - 0.5475*A*exp(-0.03708*t) + 0.7049*cos(log(A + 1))`

The GT has three basis functions:
1. `A²` (polynomial)
2. `A*exp(αt)` (exponential decay in t, multiplied by A)
3. `cos(log(A + 1))` (cosine of logarithm)

The key challenge is matching `cos(log(A+1))`. Let me check which candidates could potentially represent this.

**Key observations:**
- `cos(log(A+1))` is NOT a polynomial, NOT a rational function, NOT `log(A+1)`, NOT `sin(...)`, NOT `exp(A*c)`, NOT `sqrt(A)`, NOT a simple rational fraction `1/(A*c+d)`.
- `sin(x + π/2) = cos(x)`, so `sin(log(A+1) + π/2) = cos(log(A+1))`. But candidates with `sin(A*c + d)` have argument `A*c + d` (linear in A), NOT `log(A+1)`.
- No candidate has `cos(log(...))` or `sin(log(...))` explicitly.

Let me systematically check each candidate's basis functions:

**Candidates with `sin(A*c + d)`:** 1, 2, 16, 25, 28, 29, 30, 33, 34, 36, 37, 38, 43, 45, 47, 51, 52, 53, 55, 57
